## Page 3

### [p003_c0001] MINUTES OF THE MEETING MTA Corporate Governance Committee March 28, 2022 2 Broadway – 20 th Floor New York, New York
[p003_c0002] The following MTA Corporate Governance Committee members were present:
[p003_c0003] Hon. Janno Lieber, Chair Hon. Rhonda Herman Hon. Jamey Barbas Hon. Frank Borelli Jr. Hon. Haeda B. Mihaltses
[p003_c0004] The following MTA Corporate Governance Committee members were absent:
[p003_c0005] Hon. Kevin Law Hon. David Mack
[p003_c0006] The following non-MTA Corporate Governance Committee member was present:
[p003_c0007] Hon. Robert W. Linn
[p003_c0008] The following MTA staff attended the meeting:
[p003_c0009] Lamond W. Kearsse, Chief Compliance Officer
[p003_c0010] * * *
[p003_c0011] Chair Lieber called the March 28, 2022, meeting of the MTA Corporate Governance Committee to order at 2:36p.m.
### [p003_c0012] Public Comments Period
[p003_c0013] There were no public speakers for the public comments portion of the meeting.
### [p003_c0014] Approval of Minutes
[p003_c0015] Chair Lieber noted that the minutes of the Committee meetings held November 15, 2021, were approved at the April 2022 Board meeting.
### [p003_c0016] 1. Review and Approve Procurement Guidelines
[p003_c0017] Mr. Kearsse informed the Committee that Section 2879 of the Public Authorities Law requires the Board to annually review and approve the Procurement Guidelines and Guidelines for Procurement of Services. Mr. Kearsse informed the Board that there are only non-substantive changes since the Board last approved them.
[p003_c0018] _Master Page # 3 of 179 - Corporate Governance Committee Meeting 11/29/2022_

## Page 4

[p004_c0001] Upon motion duly made and seconded, the Committee recommended Board approval of the Procurement Guidelines and the Guidelines for Procurement of Services.
### [p004_c0002] 2. Review and Approve Mission Statement and Performance Measurement Report
[p004_c0003] Ms. Kearse advised the Committee that the Board is required to approve the MTA Mission Statement and authorized the submission of the annexed Mission Statement and Performance Indicator Report to the Authority Budget Office as required by Section 1269-f and Section 2824-a of the Public Authorities Law.
[p004_c0004] Upon motion duly made and seconded, the Committee approved the MTA Mission Statement and Performance Indicator Report to the Authority Budget Office.
### [p004_c0005] 3. Review and Approve MTA Policies in Connection with Provisions of the Public Authorities Laws
[p004_c0006] Mr. Kearse advised the Board that Section 2824 of the Public Authorities Law requires that the Board approve certain policies. The Board was presented with an exhibit book containing three (3) revised policies which have been approved by their respective Agencies.
[p004_c0007] Upon motion duly made and seconded, the Committee recommended the Board approve the policies contained in the exhibit book.
### [p004_c0008] 4. Other Business
[p004_c0009] There was no new business discussed at the meeting.
### [p004_c0010] Adjournment
[p004_c0011] Chair Lieber adjourned the March 28, meeting of the Corporate Governance Committee at 2:38pm.
[p004_c0012] Respectfully submitted
[p004_c0013] Lamond W. Kearse MTA Chief Compliance Officer
[p004_c0014] _Master Page # 4 of 179 - Corporate Governance Committee Meeting 11/29/2022_

## Page 6

### [p006_c0001] BY-LAWS MTA CONSTRUCTION AND DEVELOPMENT COMPANY
### [p006_c0002] ARTICLE 1. OFFICES
[p006_c0003] The principal office of the MTA Construction and Development Company (the "Company") shall be located in the City of New York, County of New York. The Company may have such other offices as the board may designate or as the business of the Company may require from time to time.
### [p006_c0004] ARTICLE II. THE BOARD
[p006_c0005] Section 1. General Affairs. The business and affairs of the Company shall be managed by its board.
[p006_c0006] Section 2. Number, Tenure and Qualifications. The Company ("the board" or "the board of the Company") as used herein shall consist of all of those persons who from time to time hold office as chairman or members of the Metropolitan Transportation Authority pursuant to §1263 of the Public Authorities Law of the State of New York. Each member shall hold office for the term established by law and until his successor shall have been appointed and qualified. Members shall meet all requirements of law respecting their qualification for office.
[p006_c0007] Section 3. Regular Meetings. Regular meetings of the board shall be held without other notice than these by-laws at 10:00 A.M. on the fourth Wednesday of each month except that there shall be no regular meeting in the month of August and except that in the months of November and December the regular meetings shall be held on the third Wednesday of the month. The board may provide by resolution for the time and place for the holding of additional regular meetings without other notice than such resolution. The chairman may adjust the date and time of any regular meeting by written notice provided to members at least forty-eight hours prior to such adjusted date and time. Such written notice shall be provided to members by the same means required by Section 4(b) of Article II of these by-Laws for delivery of notice to members of special meetings.
[p006_c0008] Section 4. Special Meetings. (a) Special meetings of the board may be called by the chairman or, in his or her absence or in case of his or her disability, a vice chairman. In addition, a special meeting of the board shall be called by the secretary or in his or her absence by an assistant secretary upon the request of any two members. The person or persons authorized to call special meetings of the board may fix the time and any place within the City of New York as the place for holding any special meeting of the board called or requested by them.
[p006_c0009] (b) Written notice of each special meeting shall be given by the chairman or secretary or by an assistant secretary, specifying the time and place of the meeting. Such notice shall be addressed to each member at the
[p006_c0010] _MTA Capital Construction Company Approved by the Board December 18, 2019_
[p006_c0011] _1_
[p006_c0012] _Master Page # 6 of 179 - Corporate Governance Committee Meeting 11/29/2022_

## Page 7

[p007_c0001] member's postal address on record with the Company and deposited with the U.S. Postal Service at least forty-eight hours prior to the time fixed for such meeting, and in addition, sent by facsimile or email to each member having a facsimile number or email address on record with the Company at least forty-eight hours prior to the time fixed for such special meeting. Such notice shall state the purpose of such meeting, and no business other than that stated in the notice shall be transacted at such special meeting unless every member of the Company then in office is present, and it is unanimously agreed to consider matters other than those specifically provided for in the notice of such meeting. Notwithstanding the foregoing, in the event of an emergency the chairman may call a special meeting without advance notice and by means other than the delivery of a writing to the members.
[p007_c0002] Section 5. Open Meetings. All meetings of the board shall be conducted in compliance with the provisions of the Open Meetings Law, being Chapter 511 of the Laws of 1976, as amended, and with all rules and regulations promulgated thereunder.
[p007_c0003] Section 6. Quorum. A majority of the whole number of voting members of the board as defined in §1263 (1) (a) of the Public Authorities Law of the State of New York then in office shall constitute a quorum for the transaction of any business or the exercise of any power of the Company. Those members of the board appointed upon the recommendation of the chief executive officers of Dutchess, Orange, Putnam and Rockland counties (the "Hudson Valley Member" or "Hudson Valley Members") shall be considered to be a single member, and the presence of that member for purposes of determining a quorum shall be ascertained pursuant to section 10 of this article. Except as otherwise specified by law, for the transaction of any business or exercise of any power of the Company, the Company shall have power to act by a majority of the voting members of the board present at any meeting at which a quorum is in attendance with the chairman having one additional vote in the event of a tie vote. For purposes of determining a tie vote, an abstention shall be counted as a vote against a motion. If a meeting is validly called but a quorum is not present, a majority of the members of the board then present may adjourn the meeting from time to time without further notice.
[p007_c0004] Section 7. Attendance at Meetings. (a) Any one or more members of the board or of a committee thereof may attend a meeting of such board or committee by means of a conference telephone or similar communications equipment allowing all persons attending the meeting to hear each other at the same time; however, attendance by such means shall not constitute presence at a meeting for the purposes of section 6, section 8 or section 10 of this Article.
[p007_c0005] (b) Notwithstanding the provisions of Section 7(a), a member's attendance by means of videoconferencing shall constitute presence at a meeting for any purposes of this Article, provided (i) the public notice given for
[p007_c0006] _MTA Capital Construction Company Approved by the Board December 18, 2019_
[p007_c0007] _2_
[p007_c0008] _Master Page # 7 of 179 - Corporate Governance Committee Meeting 11/29/2022_

## Page 8

[p008_c0001] such a meeting of such board or committee states that videoconferencing would be used to conduct the meeting and identifies each location at which members may attend the meeting; and (ii) at each such location, opportunity for public attendance at the meeting is provided.
[p008_c0002] Section 8. Presumption of Assent. A member of the board who is present at a meeting of the board at which action on any matter is taken shall be presumed to have assented to the action taken unless his abstention or dissent is stated at the meeting, which dissent or abstention shall be duly entered in the minutes of the meeting.
[p008_c0003] Section 9. Committees. The chairman may establish one or more committees of the board, each committee to consist of one or more of the members and each of which committees shall have and may exercise the powers conferred upon it by the chairman. Such committees shall have such names as shall be given them by the chairman. The chairman shall also establish such committees of the board as shall be mandated by law. Except in an emergency, the chairman and each board member shall be given advance written notice of the time and place of any meeting of any committee of the board.
### [p008_c0004] Section 10. Quorum and Voting for members of the Board from the counties of Dutchess, Orange, Putnam and Rockland.
[p008_c0005] (a) The Hudson Valley Members shall be considered to be a single member. For the purposes of determining a quorum, such single voting member shall be considered present if one or more Hudson Valley Members is present.
[p008_c0006] (b) The single collective vote of the Hudson Valley Members shall be determined as follows:
[p008_c0007] (i) if at least three Hudson Valley Members are then in office: (A) if one such member is present, the single collective vote shall be recognized; (B) if two or more such members are present but only one such member votes, the single collective vote shall be recognized as the vote of such member; (C) if two or more such members are present and two or more such members vote, the majority vote shall be recognized as the single collective vote; and (D) if two or more such members are present and two or more of such members vote but no majority is achieved, the single collective vote shall not be recognized; and
[p008_c0008] (ii) if two or one Hudson Valley Member(s) are then in office: (A) if one such member is present, the single collective vote shall be recognized as the vote of such voting member; (B) if two such members are present but only one such member votes, the single collective vote shall be recognized as the vote of such voting member; and (C) if two such members are present and both vote, only a unanimous vote shall be recognized as the single collective vote.
[p008_c0009] _MTA Capital Construction Company Approved by the Board December 18, 2019_
[p008_c0010] _3_
[p008_c0011] _Master Page # 8 of 179 - Corporate Governance Committee Meeting 11/29/2022_

## Page 9

[p009_c0001] To evidence the single collective vote, each such member that is present may be polled as to his vote and such poll shall be recorded in the minutes.
### [p009_c0002] ARTICLE III. OFFICERS
[p009_c0003] Section 1. Number. The officers of the Company shall be a chairman, one or more vice chairmen (the number and exact designation thereof and the separate functions to be determined by the board if there is more than one), an executive director, if one is appointed by the chairman, a president, a counsel, other senior officials (the number and exact designation thereof and the separate functions to be determined by the chairman), and a secretary. The chairman shall be appointed and shall serve as provided by law. The vice chairmen shall be appointed by the board, upon recommendation by the Chairman, and shall serve at its pleasure. The executive director, if one is appointed by the chairman, and the president shall serve at the pleasure of the chairman. Other senior officials, the counsel, and the secretary shall be appointed by the chairman and shall serve at the pleasure of the chairman. Such other officials or employees as may be deemed necessary may be appointed by the chairman, and each shall serve at the pleasure of the chairman.
[p009_c0004] Section 2. Chairman. (a) The chairman shall serve as the chairman of the board of the Company and as the chief executive officer of the Company. The chairman shall be responsible for providing leadership to the board as it oversees the management of the Company. The chairman shall preside at all meetings of the board. The chairman may delegate any or all of his or her powers relating to the leadership of the board to a vice-chairman. In the event of a tie vote, the chairman may cast an additional vote.
[p009_c0005] (b) The chairman shall also serve as the chief executive officer of the Company. As chief executive officer of the Company, the chairman shall be responsible for the discharge of the executive and administrative functions and powers of the Company.
[p009_c0006] Section 3. The Vice Chairman. In the event of the chairman's death or inability to act, or in the event the position of chairman is for any other reason vacant, a vice chairman designated by the board shall perform the duties of the chairman and when so acting, shall have all the powers of and be subject to all the restrictions upon the chairman. Such powers and duties shall terminate upon the appointment by the Governor of a successor chairman as provided by law or upon the cessation of the chairman's inability to act.
[p009_c0007] Section 4. Such Other Officials and Employees. The chairman may, in his or her judgment, appoint such other officials and employees, including an executive director, as shall in his or her judgment be needed to discharge the executive and administrative functions and powers of the Company. The chairman may delegate such of his or her powers relating to the discharge of the executive and
[p009_c0008] _MTA Capital Construction Company Approved by the Board December 18, 2019_
[p009_c0009] _4_
[p009_c0010] _Master Page # 9 of 179 - Corporate Governance Committee Meeting 11/29/2022_

## Page 10

[p010_c0001] administrative functions, including the administration and day to day operations of the Company as the chairman may deem appropriate to such other officials and employees.
[p010_c0002] Section 5. The President. The president shall have primary responsibility for the general management and operation of the Company and shall have such additional executive and administrative functions and powers as may be delegated to him or her by the chairman.
[p010_c0003] Section 6. The Secretary. The secretary shall keep the minutes of the proceedings of the board, see that all notices are duly given as required by law, be custodian of the corporate records and of the seal of the Company, see to it that the seal of the Company is affixed to all documents the execution of which on behalf of the Company under its seal is duly authorized, and in general shall perform all duties incident to the office of secretary. The chairman may appoint one or more assistant secretaries who may perform the duties of the secretary in the event of the absence, disability or incapacity of the secretary.
[p010_c0004] Section 7. Salaries. The salaries fixed by the chairman for those officers and employees appointed by the chairman shall at all times be within the amounts budgeted therefore by the board.
### [p010_c0005] ARTICLE IV. CONTRACTS, LOANS, CHECKS AND DEPOSITS
[p010_c0006] Section 1. Contracts. The board may authorize any officer or officers, agent or agents, to enter into any contract or execute and deliver any instrument in the name of and on behalf of the Company, and such authority may be general or confined to specific instances.
[p010_c0007] Section 2. Loans. No loans shall be contracted on behalf of the Company and no evidences of indebtedness shall be issued in its name unless authorized by a resolution of the board. Such authority may be general or confined to specific instances.
[p010_c0008] Section 3. Checks, Drafts, etc. All checks, drafts or other orders for the payment of money, notes or other evidences of indebtedness issued in the name of the Company shall be signed by such officer or officers, agent or agents of the Company and in such manner as shall from time to time be determined by resolution of the board.
[p010_c0009] Section 4. Deposits. All funds of the Company not otherwise employed shall be deposited from time to time to the credit of the Company in such banks, trust companies or other depositories as the board may select.
[p010_c0010] _MTA Capital Construction Company Approved by the Board December 18, 2019_
[p010_c0011] _5_
[p010_c0012] _Master Page # 10 of 179 - Corporate Governance Committee Meeting 11/29/2022_

## Page 11

### [p011_c0001] ARTICLE V. FISCAL YEAR
[p011_c0002] The fiscal year of the Company shall begin on the first day of January and end on the thirty-first day of December in each year.
### [p011_c0003] ARTICLE VI. CORPORATE SEAL
[p011_c0004] The board shall provide a corporate seal which shall be circular in form and shall have inscribed thereon the name of the Company and the words "Corporate Seal".
### [p011_c0005] ARTICLE VII. INDEMNIFICATION
[p011_c0006] The Company shall save harmless and indemnify any person (or his or her estate) who shall have served as a member, officer or employee of the Company or of a subsidiary of the Company against financial loss, including punitive damages, or litigation expense incurred in connection with any claim, demand, suit, action or proceeding, whether civil or criminal, or the defense thereof, and arising out of (a) any transaction of the Company or of a subsidiary of the Company, or (b) any act or failure to act by any such member, officer or employee while engaged in the discharge of his or her duties on behalf of the Company or its subsidiaries, or the discharge of his or her duties as a fiduciary of a benefit plan for Company employees or employees of a subsidiary of the Company. In the event any such claim, demand, suit, action or proceeding shall occur, such member, officer or employee shall be saved harmless and indemnified as herein provided unless such individual is determined by the Company or its designee not to have acted, in good faith, for a purpose which he or she reasonably believed to be in the best interests of the Company or of its subsidiaries or affiliates, and, in criminal actions or proceedings, in addition, not to have had reasonable cause to believe that his or her conduct was lawful. The provisions of this Article shall inure only to the members, officers and employees of the Company or of its subsidiaries, and to their estates, shall not enlarge or diminish the rights of any other party, and shall not impair, limit or modify the rights and obligations of any insurer under any policy of insurance. The foregoing shall be conditional on (a) the prompt delivery to the Company of a copy of the summons, complaint, process, notice, demand or pleading commencing any such claim, demand, suit, action or proceeding; and, in civil cases only, (b) a contemporaneous offer to name counsel to the Company as counsel to the member, officer or employee in the defense of such claim, demand, suit, action or proceeding; (c) the full cooperation of the member, officer or employee, in the event the offer is accepted, in making of such defense; and (d) an agreement that the Company may enter into a settlement on behalf of the member, officer or employee. If the Company or its designee determines that the defense shall not be provided by counsel for the Company because of a conflict of interests or other grounds warranting separate counsel, the member, officer or employee may select another attorney and the Company shall pay reasonable
[p011_c0007] _MTA Capital Construction Company Approved by the Board December 18, 2019_
[p011_c0008] _6_
[p011_c0009] _Master Page # 11 of 179 - Corporate Governance Committee Meeting 11/29/2022_

## Page 12

[p012_c0001] attorney's fees and expenses incurred by or on behalf of such member, officer or employee represented by outside counsel. The Company's payment of such fees and expenses may be conditioned upon the member, officer or employee's agreement that more than one member, officer or employee shall be represented by the same counsel. The provisions of Section 18 of the Public Officers Law relating to defense and indemnification shall supplement and be available in addition to the provisions of this Article; provided, however, that in the event of any conflict between the substantive provisions of this Article and those of Section 18 of the Public Officers Law, the provisions that afford the greater protection to such members, officers and employees shall control. In the event that the chairman or other member requests indemnification under this by-law, the counsel for the Authority shall review and act upon such request; provided that if upon review, the counsel believes that the facts and circumstances warrant denial of such request or raise serious question as to whether the requestor is entitled to indemnification under the by-law, such request shall be submitted to the board for determination. In the event that an officer or employee, other than the chairman, requests indemnification under this by-law, the counsel for the Authority shall review and act upon such request; provided that if upon review, the counsel believes that the facts and circumstances warrant denial of such request or raise serious question as to whether the requestor may be entitled to indemnification under the by-law, such request shall be submitted to the chairman or his or her designee for determination. The provisions of this Article replace and supersede the provisions of the prior Article VII governing Indemnification, and govern any claim, demand, suit, action or proceeding that is pending as of the date of the adoption of this Article.
### [p012_c0002] ARTICLE VIII. AMENDMENTS
[p012_c0003] These by-laws may be altered, amended or repealed and new by-laws may be adopted by the board at any regular or special meeting as to which nature of the proposed alterations, amendments or repeals have been sent in writing to the members of the board together with the notice of meeting if it is a special meeting or if at a regular meeting at least seventy-two hours in advance of such regular meeting.
[p012_c0004] _MTA Capital Construction Company Approved by the Board December 18, 2019_

## Page 13

### [p013_c0001] BY-LAWS FIRST MUTUAL TRANSPORTATION ASSURANCE COMPANY
### [p013_c0002] ARTICLE 1. OFFICES
[p013_c0003] The principal office of the First Mutual Transportation Assurance Company (the "Company") shall be located in the City of New York, County of New York. The Company may have such other offices as the board may designate or as the business of the Company may require from time to time.
### [p013_c0004] ARTICLE II. THE BOARD
[p013_c0005] Section 1. General Affairs. The business and affairs of the Company shall be managed by its board.
[p013_c0006] Section 2. Number, Tenure and Qualifications. The Company ("the board" or "the board of the Company") as used herein shall consist of all of those persons who from time to time hold office as chairman or members of the Metropolitan Transportation Authority pursuant to §1263 of the Public Authorities Law of the State of New York. Each member shall hold office for the term established by law and until his successor shall have been appointed and qualified. Members shall meet all requirements of law respecting their qualification for office.
[p013_c0007] Section 3. Regular Meetings. Regular meetings of the board shall be held without other notice than these by-laws at 10:00 A.M. on the fourth Wednesday of each month except that there shall be no regular meeting in the month of August and except that in the months of November and December the regular meetings shall be held on the third Wednesday of the month. The board may provide by resolution for the time and place for the holding of additional regular meetings without other notice than such resolution. The chairman may adjust the date and time of any regular meeting by written notice provided to members at least forty-eight hours prior to such adjusted date and time. Such written notice shall be provided to members by the same means required by Section 4(b) of Article II of these by-Laws for delivery of notice to members of special meetings. At least one meeting of the board in each year shall be held in New York State.
[p013_c0008] Section 4. Special Meetings. (a) Special meetings of the board may be called by the chairman or, in his or her absence or in case of his or her disability, a vice chairman. In addition, a special meeting of the board shall be called by the secretary or in his or her absence by an assistant secretary upon the request of any two members. The person or persons authorized to call special meetings of the board may fix the time and any place within the City of New York as the place for holding any special meeting of the board called or requested by them.
[p013_c0009] (b) Written notice of each special meeting shall be given by the chairman or secretary or by an assistant secretary, specifying the time and place
[p013_c0010] _First Mutual Transportation Assurance Company Approved by the Board July 24, 2013_
[p013_c0011] _1_
[p013_c0012] _Master Page # 13 of 179 - Corporate Governance Committee Meeting 11/29/2022_

## Page 14

[p014_c0001] of the meeting. Such notice shall be addressed to each member at the member's postal address on record with the Company and deposited with the U.S. Postal Service at least forty-eight hours prior to the time fixed for such meeting, and in addition, sent by facsimile or email to each member having a facsimile number or email address on record with the Company at least forty-eight hours prior to the time fixed for such special meeting. Such notice shall state the purpose of such meeting, and no business other than that stated in the notice shall be transacted at such special meeting unless every member of the Company then in office is present, and it is unanimously agreed to consider matters other than those specifically provided for in the notice of such meeting. Notwithstanding the foregoing, in the event of an emergency the chairman may call a special meeting without advance notice and by means other than the delivery of a writing to the members.
[p014_c0002] Section 5. Open Meetings. All meetings of the board shall be conducted in compliance with the provisions of the Open Meetings Law, being Chapter 511 of the Laws of 1976, as amended, and with all rules and regulations promulgated thereunder.
[p014_c0003] Section 6. Quorum. A majority of the whole number of voting members of the board as defined in §1263 (1) (a) of the Public Authorities Law of the State of New York then in office shall constitute a quorum for the transaction of any business or the exercise of any power of the Company. Those members of the board appointed upon the recommendation of the chief executive officers of Dutchess, Orange, Putnam and Rockland counties (the "Hudson Valley Member" or "Hudson Valley Members") shall be considered to be a single member, and the presence of that member for purposes of determining a quorum shall be ascertained pursuant to section 10 of this article. Except as otherwise specified by law, for the transaction of any business or exercise of any power of the Company, the Company shall have power to act by a majority of the voting members of the board present at any meeting at which a quorum is in attendance with the chairman having one additional vote in the event of a tie vote. For purposes of determining a tie vote, an abstention shall be counted as a vote against a motion. If a meeting is validly called but a quorum is not present, a majority of the members of the board then present may adjourn the meeting from time to time without further notice.
[p014_c0004] Section 7. Attendance at Meetings. (a) Any one or more members of the board or of a committee thereof may attend a meeting of such board or committee by means of a conference telephone or similar communications equipment allowing all persons attending the meeting to hear each other at the same time; however, attendance by such means shall not constitute presence at a meeting for the purposes of section 6, section 8 or section 10 of this Article.
[p014_c0005] (b) Notwithstanding the provisions of Section 7(a), a member's attendance by means of videoconferencing shall constitute presence at a
[p014_c0006] _First Mutual Transportation Assurance Company Approved by the Board July 24, 2013_
[p014_c0007] _2_
[p014_c0008] _Master Page # 14 of 179 - Corporate Governance Committee Meeting 11/29/2022_

## Page 15

[p015_c0001] meeting for any purposes of this Article, provided (i) the public notice given for such a meeting of such board or committee states that videoconferencing would be used to conduct the meeting and identifies each location at which members may attend the meeting; and (ii) at each such location, opportunity for public attendance at the meeting is provided.
[p015_c0002] Section 8. Presumption of Assent. A member of the board who is present at a meeting of the board at which action on any matter is taken shall be presumed to have assented to the action taken unless his abstention or dissent is stated at the meeting, which dissent or abstention shall be duly entered in the minutes of the meeting.
[p015_c0003] Section 9. Committees. The chairman may establish one or more committees of the board, each committee to consist of one or more of the members and each of which committees shall have and may exercise the powers conferred upon it by the chairman. Such committees shall have such names as shall be given them by the chairman. The chairman shall also establish such committees of the board as shall be mandated by law. Except in an emergency, the chairman and each board member shall be given advance written notice of the time and place of any meeting of any committee of the board.
### [p015_c0004] Section 10. Quorum and Voting for members of the Board from the counties of Dutchess, Orange, Putnam and Rockland.
[p015_c0005] (a) The Hudson Valley Members shall be considered to be a single member. For the purposes of determining a quorum, such single voting member shall be considered present if one or more Hudson Valley Members is present.
[p015_c0006] (b) The single collective vote of the Hudson Valley Members shall be determined as follows:
[p015_c0007] (i) if at least three Hudson Valley Members are then in office: (A) if one such member is present, the single collective vote shall be recognized; (B) if two or more such members are present but only one such member votes, the single collective vote shall be recognized as the vote of such member; (C) if two or more such members are present and two or more such members vote, the majority vote shall be recognized as the single collective vote; and (D) if two or more such members are present and two or more of such members vote but no majority is achieved, the single collective vote shall not be recognized; and
[p015_c0008] (ii) if two or one Hudson Valley Member(s) are then in office: (A) if one such member is present, the single collective vote shall be recognized as the vote of such voting member; (B) if two such members are present but only one such member votes, the single collective vote shall be recognized as the vote of such voting member; and (C) if two such members are present and both vote, only a unanimous vote shall be recognized as the single collective vote.
[p015_c0009] _First Mutual Transportation Assurance Company Approved by the Board July 24, 2013_
[p015_c0010] _3_
[p015_c0011] _Master Page # 15 of 179 - Corporate Governance Committee Meeting 11/29/2022_

## Page 16

[p016_c0001] To evidence the single collective vote, each such member that is present may be polled as to his vote and such poll shall be recorded in the minutes.
### [p016_c0002] ARTICLE III. OFFICERS
[p016_c0003] Section 1. Number. The officers of the Company shall be a chairman, one or more vice chairmen (the number and exact designation thereof and the separate functions to be determined by the board if there is more than one), an executive director, if one is appointed by the chairman, a president, a counsel, other senior officials (the number and exact designation thereof and the separate functions to be determined by the chairman), and a secretary. The chairman shall be appointed and shall serve as provided by law. The vice chairmen shall be appointed by the board, upon recommendation by the Chairman, and shall serve at its pleasure. The executive director, if one is appointed by the chairman, and the president shall serve at the pleasure of the chairman. Other senior officials, the counsel, and the secretary shall be appointed by the chairman and shall serve at the pleasure of the chairman. Such other officials or employees as may be deemed necessary may be appointed by the chairman, and each shall serve at the pleasure of the chairman.
[p016_c0004] Section 2. Chairman. (a) The chairman shall serve as the chairman of the board of the Company and as the chief executive officer of the Company. The chairman shall be responsible for providing leadership to the board as it oversees the management of the Company. The chairman shall preside at all meetings of the board. The chairman may delegate any or all of his or her powers relating to the leadership of the board to a vice-chairman. In the event of a tie vote, the chairman may cast an additional vote.
[p016_c0005] (b) The chairman shall also serve as the chief executive officer of the Company. As chief executive officer of the Company, the chairman shall be responsible for the discharge of the executive and administrative functions and powers of the Company.
[p016_c0006] Section 3. The Vice Chairman. In the event of the chairman's death or inability to act, or in the event the position of chairman is for any other reason vacant, a vice chairman designated by the board shall perform the duties of the chairman and when so acting, shall have all the powers of and be subject to all the restrictions upon the chairman. Such powers and duties shall terminate upon the appointment by the Governor of a successor chairman as provided by law or upon the cessation of the chairman's inability to act.
[p016_c0007] Section 4. Such Other Officials and Employees. The chairman may, in his or her judgment, appoint such other officials and employees, including an executive director, as shall in his or her judgment be needed to discharge the executive and administrative functions and powers of the Company. The chairman may
[p016_c0008] _First Mutual Transportation Assurance Company Approved by the Board July 24, 2013_
[p016_c0009] _4_
[p016_c0010] _Master Page # 16 of 179 - Corporate Governance Committee Meeting 11/29/2022_

## Page 17

[p017_c0001] delegate such of his or her powers relating to the discharge of the executive and administrative functions, including the administration and day to day operations of the Company as the chairman may deem appropriate to such other officials and employees.
[p017_c0002] Section 5. The President. The president shall have primary responsibility for the general management and operation of the Company and shall have such additional executive and administrative functions and powers as may be delegated to him or her by the chairman.
[p017_c0003] Section 6. The Secretary. The secretary shall keep the minutes of the proceedings of the board, see that all notices are duly given as required by law, be custodian of the corporate records and of the seal of the Company, see to it that the seal of the Company is affixed to all documents the execution of which on behalf of the Company under its seal is duly authorized, and in general shall perform all duties incident to the office of secretary. The chairman may appoint one or more assistant secretaries who may perform the duties of the secretary in the event of the absence, disability or incapacity of the secretary.
[p017_c0004] Section 7. Salaries. The salaries fixed by the chairman for those officers and employees appointed by the chairman shall at all times be within the amounts budgeted therefore by the board.
### [p017_c0005] ARTICLE IV. CONTRACTS, LOANS, CHECKS AND DEPOSITS
[p017_c0006] Section 1. Contracts. The board may authorize any officer or officers, agent or agents, to enter into any contract or execute and deliver any instrument in the name of and on behalf of the Company, and such authority may be general or confined to specific instances.
[p017_c0007] Section 2. Loans. No loans shall be contracted on behalf of the Company and no evidences of indebtedness shall be issued in its name unless authorized by a resolution of the board. Such authority may be general or confined to specific instances.
[p017_c0008] Section 3. Checks, Drafts, etc. All checks, drafts or other orders for the payment of money, notes or other evidences of indebtedness issued in the name of the Company shall be signed by such officer or officers, agent or agents of the Company and in such manner as shall from time to time be determined by resolution of the board.
[p017_c0009] Section 4. Deposits. All funds of the Company not otherwise employed shall be deposited from time to time to the credit of the Company in such banks, trust companies or other depositories as the board may select.

### [p018_c0001] ARTICLE V. FISCAL YEAR
[p018_c0002] The fiscal year of the Company shall begin on the first day of January and end on the thirty-first day of December in each year.
### [p018_c0003] ARTICLE VI. CORPORATE SEAL
[p018_c0004] The board shall provide a corporate seal which shall be circular in form and shall have inscribed thereon the name of the Company and the words "Corporate Seal".
### [p018_c0005] ARTICLE VII. INDEMNIFICATION
[p018_c0006] The Company shall save harmless and indemnify any person (or his or her estate) who shall have served as a member, officer or employee of the Company or of a subsidiary of the Company against financial loss, including punitive damages, or litigation expense incurred in connection with any claim, demand, suit, action or proceeding, whether civil or criminal, or the defense thereof, and arising out of (a) any transaction of the Company or of a subsidiary of the Company, or (b) any act or failure to act by any such member, officer or employee while engaged in the discharge of his or her duties on behalf of the Company or its subsidiaries, or the discharge of his or her duties as a fiduciary of a benefit plan for Company employees or employees of a subsidiary of the Company. In the event any such claim, demand, suit, action or proceeding shall occur, such member, officer or employee shall be saved harmless and indemnified as herein provided unless such individual is determined by the Company or its designee not to have acted, in good faith, for a purpose which he or she reasonably believed to be in the best interests of the Company or of its subsidiaries or affiliates, and, in criminal actions or proceedings, in addition, not to have had reasonable cause to believe that his or her conduct was lawful. The provisions of this Article shall inure only to the members, officers and employees of the Company or of its subsidiaries, and to their estates, shall not enlarge or diminish the rights of any other party, and shall not impair, limit or modify the rights and obligations of any insurer under any policy of insurance. The foregoing shall be conditional on (a) the prompt delivery to the Company of a copy of the summons, complaint, process, notice, demand or pleading commencing any such claim, demand, suit, action or proceeding; and, in civil cases only, (b) a contemporaneous offer to name counsel to the Company as counsel to the member, officer or employee in the defense of such claim, demand, suit, action or proceeding; (c) the full cooperation of the member, officer or employee, in the event the offer is accepted, in making of such defense; and (d) an agreement that the Company may enter into a settlement on behalf of the member, officer or employee. If the Company or its designee determines that the defense shall not be provided by counsel for the Company because of a conflict of interests or other grounds warranting separate counsel, the member, officer or employee may select another attorney and the Company shall pay reasonable
[p018_c0007] _First Mutual Transportation Assurance Company Approved by the Board July 24, 2013_
[p018_c0008] _6_
[p018_c0009] _Master Page # 18 of 179 - Corporate Governance Committee Meeting 11/29/2022_

## Page 19

[p019_c0001] attorney's fees and expenses incurred by or on behalf of such member, officer or employee represented by outside counsel. The Company's payment of such fees and expenses may be conditioned upon the member, officer or employee's agreement that more than one member, officer or employee shall be represented by the same counsel. The provisions of Section 18 of the Public Officers Law relating to defense and indemnification shall supplement and be available in addition to the provisions of this Article; provided, however, that in the event of any conflict between the substantive provisions of this Article and those of Section 18 of the Public Officers Law, the provisions that afford the greater protection to such members, officers and employees shall control. In the event that the chairman or other member requests indemnification under this by-law, the counsel for the Authority shall review and act upon such request; provided that if upon review, the counsel believes that the facts and circumstances warrant denial of such request or raise serious question as to whether the requestor is entitled to indemnification under the by-law, such request shall be submitted to the board for determination. In the event that an officer or employee, other than the chairman, requests indemnification under this by-law, the counsel for the Authority shall review and act upon such request; provided that if upon review, the counsel believes that the facts and circumstances warrant denial of such request or raise serious question as to whether the requestor may be entitled to indemnification under the by-law, such request shall be submitted to the chairman or his or her designee for determination. The provisions of this Article replace and supersede the provisions of the prior Article VII governing Indemnification, and govern any claim, demand, suit, action or proceeding that is pending as of the date of the adoption of this Article.
### [p019_c0002] ARTICLE VIII. AMENDMENTS
[p019_c0003] These by-laws may be altered, amended or repealed and new by-laws may be adopted by the board at any regular or special meeting as to which nature of the proposed alterations, amendments or repeals have been sent in writing to the members of the board together with the notice of meeting if it is a special meeting or if at a regular meeting at least seventy-two hours in advance of such regular meeting.

### [p020_c0004] ARTICLE II. THE BOARD
[p020_c0005] Section 1. General Affairs. The business and affairs of the Company shall be managed by its board.
[p020_c0006] Section 2. Number, Tenure and Qualifications. The Company (“the board” or “the board of the company”) as used herein shall consist of all of those persons who from time to time hold office as chairman or members of the Metropolitan Transportation Authority pursuant to §1263 of the Public Authorities Law of the State of New York. Each member shall hold office for the term established by law and until his successor shall have been appointed and qualified. Board members shall meet all requirements of law respecting their qualification for office.
[p020_c0007] Section 3. Regular Meetings. Regular meetings of the board shall be held without other notice than these by-laws at 10:00 A.M. on the fourth Wednesday of each month except that there shall be no regular meeting in the month of August and except that in the months of November and December the regular meetings shall be held on the third Wednesday of the month. The board may provide by resolution for the time and place for the holding of additional regular meetings without other notice than such resolution. In addition, a special meeting of the board shall be called by the secretary or in their absence by an assistant secretary upon the request of any two members. The person or persons authorized to call special meetings of the board may fix the time and any place within the City of New York as the place for holding any special meeting of the board called or requested by them.

In addition, the notice shall be sent by email to each member having an email address on record with the Company and such email shall be sent at least forty-eight hours prior to the time fixed for such special meeting. The notice shall state the purpose of the special meeting. No business other than that stated in the notice shall be transacted at the special meeting unless every member of the Company then in office is present and it is unanimously agreed to consider matters other than those specifically provided for in the notice of such meeting. [p021_c0003] Section 6. Quorum. A majority of the whole number of voting members of the board, as defined in §1263 (1) (a) of the Public Authorities Law of the State of New York, then in office shall constitute a quorum for the transaction of any business or the exercise of any power of the Company. For purposes of determining a tie vote, an abstention shall be counted as a vote against a motion. [p021_c0004] Section 7. Attendance at Meetings. Any one or more members of the board or of a committee thereof may attend a meeting of such board or committee by means of a conference telephone or similar communications equipment allowing all persons attending the meeting to hear each other at the same time; however, attendance by such means shall not constitute presence at a meeting for the purposes of section 6, section 8 or section 10 of this Article.

[p022_c0001] Notwithstanding the aforementioned language, a member's attendance by means of videoconferencing shall constitute presence at a meeting for any purposes of this Article provided: (i) the public notice given for such a meeting of such board or committee states that videoconferencing would be used to conduct the meeting and identifies each location at which members may attend the meeting; and (ii) at each such location, opportunity for public attendance at the meeting is provided.

### [p023_c0003] ARTICLE III. OFFICERS
[p023_c0004] Section 1. Number. In the event of a tie vote, the chairman may cast an additional vote.

[p023_c0007] Section 3. The Vice Chairman. In the event of the chairman's death or inability to act, or in the event the position of chairman is for any other reason vacant, a vice chairman designated by the board shall perform the duties of the chairman and when so acting, shall have all the powers of and be subject to all the restrictions upon the chairman. Such powers and duties shall terminate upon the appointment by the Governor of a successor chairman as provided by law or upon the cessation of the chairman's inability to act.

[p024_c0001] Section 4. Such Other Officials and Employees. The chairman may delegate such of their powers relating to the discharge of the executive and administrative functions, including the administration and day to day operations of the Company as the chairman may deem appropriate to such other officials and employees.
[p024_c0002] Section 5. The President. The president shall have primary responsibility for the general management and operation of the Company and shall have such additional executive and administrative functions and powers as may be delegated to him or her by the chairman.
[p024_c0003] Section 6. The Secretary. The secretary shall keep the minutes of the proceedings of the board, see that all notices are duly given as required by law, be custodian of the corporate records and of the seal of the Company, see to it that the seal of the Company is affixed to all documents the execution of which on behalf of the Company under its seal is duly authorized, and in general shall perform all duties incident to the office of secretary. The chairman may appoint one or more assistant secretaries who may perform the duties of the secretary in the event of the absence, disability or incapacity of the secretary.
[p024_c0004] Section 7. Salaries. The salaries fixed by the chairman for those officers and employees appointed by the chairman shall at all times be within the amounts budgeted therefore by the board.
### [p024_c0005] ARTICLE IV. CONTRACTS, LOANS, CHECKS AND DEPOSITS
[p024_c0006] Section 1. Contracts. The board may authorize any officer or officers, agent or agents, to enter into any contract or execute and deliver any instrument in the name of and on behalf of the Company, and such authority may be general or confined to specific instances.
[p024_c0007] Section 2. Loans. No loans shall be contracted on behalf of the Company and no evidences of indebtedness shall be issued in its name unless authorized by a resolution of the board. Such authority may be general or confined to specific instances.
[p024_c0008] Section 3. Checks, Drafts, and Orders for the Payment of Money or Evidences of Indebtedness. All checks, drafts or other orders for the payment of money, notes or other evidences of indebtedness issued in the name of the Company shall be signed by such officer or officers, agent or agents of the Company and in such manner as shall from time to time be determined by resolution of the board.
[p024_c0009] _MTA Grand Central Madison Concourse Operating Company Approved by the Board on October 20, 2021_
[p024_c0010] _5_
[p024_c0011] _Master Page # 24 of 179 - Corporate Governance Committee Meeting 11/29/2022_

## Page 25

[p025_c0001] Section 4. Deposits. All funds of the Company not otherwise employed shall be deposited from time to time to the credit of the Company in such banks, trust companies or other depositories as the board may select.
### [p025_c0002] ARTICLE V. FISCAL YEAR
[p025_c0003] The fiscal year of the Company shall begin on the first day of January and end on the thirty-first day of December in each year.
### [p025_c0004] ARTICLE VI. CORPORATE SEAL
[p025_c0005] The board shall provide a corporate seal which shall be circular in form and shall have inscribed thereon the name of the Company and the words “Corporate Seal”.
### [p025_c0006] ARTICLE VII. INDEMNIFICATION
[p025_c0007] The Company shall save harmless and indemnify any person (or their estate) who shall have served as a member, officer or employee of the Company or of a subsidiary of the Company against financial loss, including punitive damages, or litigation expense incurred in connection with any claim, demand, suit, action or proceeding, whether civil or criminal, or the defense thereof, and arising out of: (a) any transaction of the Company or of a subsidiary of the Company; or (b) any act or failure to act by any such member, officer or employee while engaged in the discharge of their duties on behalf of the Company or its subsidiaries, or the discharge of their duties as a fiduciary of a benefit plan for Company employees or employees of a subsidiary of the Company. In the event any such claim, demand, suit, action or proceeding shall occur, such member, officer or employee shall be saved harmless and indemnified as herein provided unless such individual is determined by the Company or its designee not to have acted, in good faith, for a purpose which they reasonably believed to be in the best interests of the Company or of its subsidiaries or affiliates, and, in criminal actions or proceedings, in addition, not to have had reasonable cause to believe that their conduct was lawful. The provisions of this Article shall inure only to the members, officers and employees of the Company or of its subsidiaries, and to their estates, shall not enlarge or diminish the rights of any other party, and shall not impair, limit or modify the rights and obligations of any insurer under any policy of insurance. The foregoing shall be conditional on: (a) the prompt delivery to the Company of a copy of the summons, complaint, process, notice, demand or pleading commencing any such claim, demand, suit, action or proceeding; and, in civil cases only; (b) a contemporaneous offer to name counsel to the Company as counsel to the member, officer or employee in the defense of such claim, demand, suit, action or proceeding; (c) the full cooperation of the member, officer or employee, in the event the offer is accepted, in making of such defense; and (d) an agreement that the Company may enter into a settlement on behalf of
[p025_c0008] _MTA Grand Central Madison Concourse Operating Company Approved by the Board on October 20, 2021_
[p025_c0009] _6_
[p025_c0010] _Master Page # 25 of 179 - Corporate Governance Committee Meeting 11/29/2022_

## Page 26

[p026_c0001] the member, officer or employee. If the Company determines that the defense shall not be provided by counsel for the Company because of a conflict of interests or other grounds warranting separate counsel, the member, officer or employee may select another attorney and the Company shall pay reasonable attorneys' fees and expenses incurred by or on behalf of such member, officer or employee represented by outside counsel. The Company's payment of such fees and expenses may be conditioned upon the member, officer or employee's agreement that more than one member, officer or employee shall be represented by the same counsel. The provisions of Section 18 of the Public Officers Law relating to defense and indemnification shall supplement and be available in addition to the provisions of this Article; provided, however, that in the event of any conflict between the substantive provisions of this Article and those of Section 18 of the Public Officers Law, the provisions that afford the greater protection to such members, officers and employees shall control. In the event that the chairman or other member requests indemnification under this by-law, the counsel for the Authority shall review and act upon such request; provided that if upon review, the counsel believes that the facts and circumstances warrant denial of such request or raise serious question as to whether the requestor is entitled to indemnification under the by-law, such request shall be submitted to the board for determination. In the event that an officer or employee, other than the chairman, requests indemnification under this by-law, the counsel for the Authority shall review and act upon such request; provided that if upon review, the counsel believes that the facts and circumstances warrant denial of such request or raise serious question as to whether the requestor may be entitled to indemnification under the by-law, such request shall be submitted to the chairman for determination. The provisions of this Article replace and supersede the provisions of the prior Article VII governing Indemnification, and govern any claim, demand, suit, action or proceeding that is pending as of the date of the adoption of this Article.
### [p026_c0002] ARTICLE VIII. AMENDMENTS
[p026_c0003] These by-laws may be altered, amended or repealed and new by-laws may be adopted by the board at any special or regular meeting. For special meetings, the proposed alterations, amendments or repeals should be sent, in writing, to the members of the board, together with the notice of meeting. For regular meetings, the same requirements apply, but the sending must occur at least seventy-two hours in advance of such regular meeting.
[p026_c0004] _MTA Grand Central Madison Concourse Operating Company Approved by the Board on October 20, 2021_
[p026_c0005] _7_

### [p027_c0001] BY-LAWS LONG ISLAND RAIL ROAD COMPANY
### [p027_c0002] ARTICLE 1. OFFICES
[p027_c0003] The principal office of the Long Island Rail Road Company (the "Rail Road") shall be located at Jamaica Station, 93-02 Sutphin Boulevard, Borough and County of Queens, City of New York. The Rail Road may have such other offices as the board may designate or as the business of the Rail Road may require from time to time.
### [p027_c0004] ARTICLE II. THE BOARD
[p027_c0005] Section 1. General Affairs. The business and affairs of the Rail Road shall be managed by its board.
[p027_c0006] Section 2. Number, Tenure and Qualifications. The Rail Road ("the board" or "the board of the Rail Road") as used herein shall consist of all of those persons who from time to time hold office as chairman or members of the Metropolitan Transportation Authority pursuant to §1263 of the Public Authorities Law of the State of New York. Each member shall hold office for the term established by law and until his successor shall have been appointed and qualified. Members shall meet all requirements of law respecting their qualification for office.
[p027_c0007] Section 3. Regular Meetings. Regular meetings of the board shall be held without other notice than these by-laws at 10:00 A.M. on the fourth Wednesday of each month except that there shall be no regular meeting in the month of August and except that in the months of November and December the regular meetings shall be held on the third Wednesday of the month. The board may provide by resolution for the time and place for the holding of additional regular meetings without other notice than such resolution. The chairman may adjust the date and time of any regular meeting by written notice provided to members at least forty-eight hours prior to such adjusted date and time. Such written notice shall be provided to members by the same means required by Section 4(b) of Article II of these by-Laws for delivery of notice to members of special meetings.
[p027_c0008] Section 4. Special Meetings. (a) Special meetings of the board may be called by the chairman or, in his or her absence or in case of his or her disability, a vice chairman. In addition, a special meeting of the board shall be called by the secretary or in his or her absence by an assistant secretary upon the request of any two members. The person or persons authorized to call special meetings of the board may fix the time and any place within the City of New York as the place for holding any special meeting of the board called or requested by them.
[p027_c0009] (b) Written notice of each special meeting shall be given by the chairman or secretary or by an assistant secretary, specifying the time and place
[p027_c0010] _Long Island Rail Road Approved by the Board July 24, 2013_
[p027_c0011] _1_
[p027_c0012] _Master Page # 27 of 179 - Corporate Governance Committee Meeting 11/29/2022_

## Page 28

[p028_c0001] of the meeting. Such notice shall be addressed to each member at the member's postal address on record with the Rail Road and deposited with the U.S. Postal Service at least forty-eight hours prior to the time fixed for such meeting, and in addition, sent by facsimile or email to each member having a facsimile number or email address on record with the Rail Road at least forty-eight hours prior to the time fixed for such special meeting. Such notice shall state the purpose of such meeting, and no business other than that stated in the notice shall be transacted at such special meeting unless every member of the Rail Road then in office is present, and it is unanimously agreed to consider matters other than those specifically provided for in the notice of such meeting. Notwithstanding the foregoing, in the event of an emergency the chairman may call a special meeting without advance notice and by means other than the delivery of a writing to the members.
[p028_c0002] Section 5. Open Meetings. All meetings of the board shall be conducted in compliance with the provisions of the Open Meetings Law, being Chapter 511 of the Laws of 1976, as amended, and with all rules and regulations promulgated thereunder.
[p028_c0003] Section 6. Quorum. A majority of the whole number of voting members of the board as defined in §1263 (1) (a) of the Public Authorities Law of the State of New York then in office shall constitute a quorum for the transaction of any business or the exercise of any power of the Rail Road. Those members of the board appointed upon the recommendation of the chief executive officers of Dutchess, Orange, Putnam and Rockland counties (the "Hudson Valley Member" or "Hudson Valley Members") shall be considered to be a single member, and the presence of that member for purposes of determining a quorum shall be ascertained pursuant to section 10 of this article. Except as otherwise specified by law, for the transaction of any business or exercise of any power of the Rail Road, the Rail Road shall have power to act by a majority of the voting members of the board present at any meeting at which a quorum is in attendance with the chairman having one additional vote in the event of a tie vote. For purposes of determining a tie vote, an abstention shall be counted as a vote against a motion. If a meeting is validly called but a quorum is not present, a majority of the members of the board then present may adjourn the meeting from time to time without further notice.
[p028_c0004] Section 7. Attendance at Meetings. (a) Any one or more members of the board or of a committee thereof may attend a meeting of such board or committee by means of a conference telephone or similar communications equipment allowing all persons attending the meeting to hear each other at the same time; however, attendance by such means shall not constitute presence at a meeting for the purposes of section 6, section 8 or section 10 of this Article.
[p028_c0005] (b) Notwithstanding the provisions of Section 7(a), a member's attendance by means of videoconferencing shall constitute presence at a
[p028_c0006] _Long Island Rail Road Approved by the Board July 24, 2013_
[p028_c0007] _2_
[p028_c0008] _Master Page # 28 of 179 - Corporate Governance Committee Meeting 11/29/2022_

## Page 29

[p029_c0001] meeting for any purposes of this Article, provided (i) the public notice given for such a meeting of such board or committee states that videoconferencing would be used to conduct the meeting and identifies each location at which members may attend the meeting; and (ii) at each such location, opportunity for public attendance at the meeting is provided.
[p029_c0002] Section 8. Presumption of Assent. A member of the board who is present at a meeting of the board at which action on any matter is taken shall be presumed to have assented to the action taken unless his abstention or dissent is stated at the meeting, which dissent or abstention shall be duly entered in the minutes of the meeting.
[p029_c0003] Section 9. Committees. The chairman may establish one or more committees of the board, each committee to consist of one or more of the members and each of which committees shall have and may exercise the powers conferred upon it by the chairman. Such committees shall have such names as shall be given them by the chairman. The chairman shall also establish such committees of the board as shall be mandated by law. Except in an emergency, the chairman and each board member shall be given advance written notice of the time and place of any meeting of any committee of the board.
[p029_c0004] Section 10. Quorum and Voting for members of the Board from the counties of Dutchess, Orange, Putnam and Rockland.
[p029_c0005] (a) The Hudson Valley Members shall be considered to be a single member. For the purposes of determining a quorum, such single voting member shall be considered present if one or more Hudson Valley Members is present.
[p029_c0006] (b) The single collective vote of the Hudson Valley Members shall be determined as follows:
[p029_c0007] (i) if at least three Hudson Valley Members are then in office: (A) if one such member is present, the single collective vote shall be recognized; (B) if two or more such members are present but only one such member votes, the single collective vote shall be recognized as the vote of such member; (C) if two or more such members are present and two or more such members vote, the majority vote shall be recognized as the single collective vote; and (D) if two or more such members are present and two or more of such members vote but no majority is achieved, the single collective vote shall not be recognized; and
[p029_c0008] (ii) if two or one Hudson Valley Member(s) are then in office: (A) if one such member is present, the single collective vote shall be recognized as the vote of such voting member; (B) if two such members are present but only one such member votes, the single collective vote shall be recognized as the vote of such voting member; and (C) if two such members are present and both vote, only a unanimous vote shall be recognized as the single collective vote.
[p029_c0009] _Long Island Rail Road Approved by the Board July 24, 2013_
[p029_c0010] _3_
[p029_c0011] _Master Page # 29 of 179 - Corporate Governance Committee Meeting 11/29/2022_

## Page 30

[p030_c0001] To evidence the single collective vote, each such member that is present may be polled as to his vote and such poll shall be recorded in the minutes.
### [p030_c0002] ARTICLE III. OFFICERS
[p030_c0003] Section 1. Number. The officers of the Rail Road shall be a chairman, one or more vice chairmen (the number and exact designation thereof and the separate functions to be determined by the board if there is more than one), an executive director, if one is appointed by the chairman, a president, a counsel, other senior officials (the number and exact designation thereof and the separate functions to be determined by the chairman), and a secretary. The chairman shall be appointed and shall serve as provided by law. The vice chairmen shall be appointed by the board, upon recommendation by the Chairman, and shall serve at its pleasure. The executive director, if one is appointed by the chairman, and the president shall serve at the pleasure of the chairman. Other senior officials, the counsel, and the secretary shall be appointed by the chairman and shall serve at the pleasure of the chairman. Such other officials or employees as may be deemed necessary may be appointed by the chairman, and each shall serve at the pleasure of the chairman.
[p030_c0004] Section 2. Chairman. (a) The chairman shall serve as the chairman of the board of the Rail Road and as the chief executive officer of the Rail Road. The chairman shall be responsible for providing leadership to the board as it oversees the management of the Rail Road. The chairman shall preside at all meetings of the board. The chairman may delegate any or all of his or her powers relating to the leadership of the board to a vice-chairman. In the event of a tie vote, the chairman may cast an additional vote.
[p030_c0005] (b) The chairman shall also serve as the chief executive officer of the Rail Road. As chief executive officer of the Rail Road, the chairman shall be responsible for the discharge of the executive and administrative functions and powers of the Rail Road.
[p030_c0006] Section 3. The Vice Chairman. In the event of the chairman's death or inability to act, or in the event the position of chairman is for any other reason vacant, a vice chairman designated by the board shall perform the duties of the chairman and when so acting, shall have all the powers of and be subject to all the restrictions upon the chairman. Such powers and duties shall terminate upon the appointment by the Governor of a successor chairman as provided by law or upon the cessation of the chairman's inability to act.
[p030_c0007] Section 4. Such Other Officials and Employees. The chairman may, in his or her judgment, appoint such other officials and employees, including an executive director, as shall in his or her judgment be needed to discharge the executive and administrative functions and powers of the Rail Road. The chairman may
[p030_c0008] _Long Island Rail Road Approved by the Board July 24, 2013_
[p030_c0009] _4_
[p030_c0010] _Master Page # 30 of 179 - Corporate Governance Committee Meeting 11/29/2022_

## Page 31

[p031_c0001] delegate such of his or her powers relating to the discharge of the executive and administrative functions, including the administration and day to day operations of the Rail Road as the chairman may deem appropriate to such other officials and employees.
[p031_c0002] Section 5. The President. The president shall have primary responsibility for the general management and operation of the Rail Road and shall have such additional executive and administrative functions and powers as may be delegated to him or her by the chairman.
[p031_c0003] Section 6. The Secretary. The secretary shall keep the minutes of the proceedings of the board, see that all notices are duly given as required by law, be custodian of the corporate records and of the seal of the Rail Road, see to it that the seal of the Rail Road is affixed to all documents the execution of which on behalf of the Rail Road under its seal is duly authorized, and in general shall perform all duties incident to the office of secretary. The chairman may appoint one or more assistant secretaries who may perform the duties of the secretary in the event of the absence, disability or incapacity of the secretary.
[p031_c0004] Section 7. Salaries. The salaries fixed by the chairman for those officers and employees appointed by the chairman shall at all times be within the amounts budgeted therefore by the board.
### [p031_c0005] ARTICLE IV. CONTRACTS, LOANS, CHECKS AND DEPOSITS
[p031_c0006] Section 1. Contracts. The board may authorize any officer or officers, agent or agents, to enter into any contract or execute and deliver any instrument in the name of and on behalf of the Rail Road, and such authority may be general or confined to specific instances.
[p031_c0007] Section 2. Loans. No loans shall be contracted on behalf of the Rail Road and no evidences of indebtedness shall be issued in its name unless authorized by a resolution of the board. Such authority may be general or confined to specific instances.
[p031_c0008] Section 3. Checks, Drafts, etc. All checks, drafts or other orders for the payment of money, notes or other evidences of indebtedness issued in the name of the Rail Road shall be signed by such officer or officers, agent or agents of the Rail Road and in such manner as shall from time to time be determined by resolution of the board.
[p031_c0009] Section 4. Deposits. All funds of the Rail Road not otherwise employed shall be deposited from time to time to the credit of the Rail Road in such banks, trust companies or other depositories as the board may select.
[p031_c0010] _Long Island Rail Road Approved by the Board July 24, 2013_

### [p032_c0001] ARTICLE V. FISCAL YEAR
[p032_c0002] The fiscal year of the Rail Road shall begin on the first day of January and end on the thirty-first day of December in each year.
### [p032_c0003] ARTICLE VI. CORPORATE SEAL
[p032_c0004] The board shall provide a corporate seal which shall be circular in form and shall have inscribed thereon the name of the Rail Road and the words "Corporate Seal".
### [p032_c0005] ARTICLE VII. INDEMNIFICATION
[p032_c0006] The Rail Road shall save harmless and indemnify any person (or his or her estate) who shall have served as a member, officer or employee of the Rail Road or of a subsidiary of the Rail Road against financial loss, including punitive damages, or litigation expense incurred in connection with any claim, demand, suit, action or proceeding, whether civil or criminal, or the defense thereof, and arising out of (a) any transaction of the Rail Road or of a subsidiary of the Rail Road, or (b) any act or failure to act by any such member, officer or employee while engaged in the discharge of his or her duties on behalf of the Rail Road or its subsidiaries, or the discharge of his or her duties as a fiduciary of a benefit plan for Rail Road employees or employees of a subsidiary of the Rail Road. In the event any such claim, demand, suit, action or proceeding shall occur, such member, officer or employee shall be saved harmless and indemnified as herein provided unless such individual is determined by the Rail Road or its designee not to have acted, in good faith, for a purpose which he or she reasonably believed to be in the best interests of the Rail Road or of its subsidiaries or affiliates, and, in criminal actions or proceedings, in addition, not to have had reasonable cause to believe that his or her conduct was lawful. The provisions of this Article shall inure only to the members, officers and employees of the Rail Road or of its subsidiaries, and to their estates, shall not enlarge or diminish the rights of any other party, and shall not impair, limit or modify the rights and obligations of any insurer under any policy of insurance. The foregoing shall be conditional on (a) the prompt delivery to the Rail Road of a copy of the summons, complaint, process, notice, demand or pleading commencing any such claim, demand, suit, action or proceeding; and, in civil cases only, (b) a contemporaneous offer to name counsel to the Rail Road as counsel to the member, officer or employee in the defense of such claim, demand, suit, action or proceeding; (c) the full cooperation of the member, officer or employee, in the event the offer is accepted, in the making of such defense; and (d) an agreement that the Rail Road may enter into a settlement on behalf of the member, officer or employee. If the Rail Road or its designee determines that the defense shall not be provided by counsel for the Rail Road because of a conflict of interests or other grounds warranting separate counsel, the member, officer or employee may select another attorney and the Rail Road shall pay reasonable attorney's
[p032_c0007] _Long Island Rail Road Approved by the Board July 24, 2013_
[p032_c0008] _6_
[p032_c0009] _Master Page # 32 of 179 - Corporate Governance Committee Meeting 11/29/2022_

## Page 33

[p033_c0001] fees and expenses incurred by or on behalf of such member, officer or employee represented by outside counsel. The Rail Road's payment of such fees and expenses may be conditioned upon the member, officer or employee's agreement that more than one member, officer or employee shall be represented by the same counsel. The provisions of Section 18 of the Public Officers Law relating to defense and indemnification shall supplement and be available in addition to the provisions of this Article; provided, however, that in the event of any conflict between the substantive provisions of this Article and those of Section 18 of the Public Officers Law, the provisions that afford the greater protection to such members, officers and employees shall control. In the event that the chairman or other member requests indemnification under this section, such request shall be submitted to the board for its determination. In the event that the chairman or other member requests indemnification under this by-law, the counsel for the Authority shall review and act upon such request; provided that if upon review, the counsel believes that the facts and circumstances warrant denial of such request or raise serious question as to whether the requestor is entitled to indemnification under the by-law, such request shall be submitted to the board for determination. In the event that an officer or employee, other than the chairman, requests indemnification under this by-law, the counsel for the Authority shall review and act upon such request; provided that if upon review, the counsel believes that the facts and circumstances warrant denial of such request or raise serious question as to whether the requestor may be entitled to indemnification under the by-law, such request shall be submitted to the chairman or his or her designee for determination. The provisions of this Article replace and supersede the provisions of the prior Article VII governing Indemnification, and govern any claim, demand, suit, action or proceeding that is pending as of the date of the adoption of this Article.
### [p033_c0002] ARTICLE VIII. AMENDMENTS
[p033_c0003] These by-laws may be altered, amended or repealed and new by-laws may be adopted by the board at any regular or special meeting as to which nature of the proposed alterations, amendments or repeals have been sent in writing to the members of the board together with the notice of meeting if it is a special meeting or if at a regular meeting at least seventy-two hours in advance of such regular meeting.
